  \"repo\": \"github.com/grafana/grafana\",\n      \"path\": \"pkg/storage/unified/migrations/table_locker.go\",\n      \"symbol\": \"MigrationTableLocker\"\n    },\n    {\n      \"repo\": \"github.com/grafana/grafana\",\n      \"path\": \"pkg/services/secrets/migrator/migrator.go\",\n      \"symbol\": \"SecretsMigrator\"\n    },\n    {\n      \"repo\": \"github.com/grafana/grafana\",\n      \"path\": \"pkg/services/secrets/migrator/rollback.go\",\n      \"symbol\": \"RollBackSecrets\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Grafana database migration framework consists of multiple integrated systems for managing database schema changes across different storage backends and secret management layers.\\n\\n## Core SQL Store Migration System (pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/)\\n\\nThe foundation of Grafana's migration framework is implemented in `migrator.go`, which provides the `Migrator` type that orchestrates the execution of migrations. The migrator:\\n- Maintains a migration log table (`migration_log`, `secret_migration_log`, `resource_migration_log`, or `unifiedstorage_migration_log`) that tracks which migrations have been applied\\n- Executes migrations sequentially based on their dependencies\\n- Supports database locking to prevent concurrent migrations\\n- Records migration results including success/failure status and timestamps\\n\\nThe `types.go` file defines core interfaces:\\n- `Migration` interface: Base interface for all migrations with `SQL(dialect)`, `Id()`, and condition methods\\n- `CodeMigration` interface: For migrations that execute custom Go code via `Exec()` method\\n- `MigrationCondition` interface: For conditional migration execution\\n\\n## SQL Dialect Abstraction (MySQL/Postgres/SQLite)\\n\\nThe dialect abstraction layer (`dialect.go`) provides a `Dialect` interface with dialect-specific implementations:\\n- `BaseDialect` provides common functionality including SQL generation for CREATE TABLE, ADD COLUMN, CREATE INDEX, etc.\\n- `mysql_dialect.go`: MySQL-specific implementation with InnoDB engine, UTF8MB4 collation support, and MySQL-specific locking\\n- `postgres_dialect.go`: PostgreSQL implementation with native UUID support and PostgreSQL-specific syntax\\n- `sqlite_dialect.go`: SQLite implementation with transaction-based locking and PRAGMA support\\n\\nEach dialect implements:\\n- `Quote()`: identifier quoting specific to the database\\n- `SQLType()`: column type mapping\\n- `CreateTableSQL()`, `AddColumnSQL()`, `CreateIndexSQL()`: SQL generation\\n- `Lock()`/`Unlock()`: database-specific locking mechanisms\\n- `CreateDatabaseFromSnapshot()`: schema recreation from snapshot files\\n\\n## Migration Definitions and Types\\n\\n`migrations.go` provides migration builders:\\n- `RawSQLMigration`: Direct SQL execution\\n- `AddTableMigration`: Table creation with dialect-specific SQL generation\\n- `AddColumnMigration`: Add column operations\\n- `DropIndexMigration`, `DropTableMigration`, etc.\\n\\nEach migration type's `SQL(dialect)` method generates database-specific SQL statements.\\n\\n## OSS Migrations Registry (pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/)\\n\\nThe `OSSMigrations` type in `migrations.go` implements the `DatabaseMigrator` interface and aggregates all migrations by calling:\\n- `addUserMigrations()`, `addDashboardMigration()`, `addDataSourceMigration()`, etc.\\n- Each adds migrations to the `Migrator` instance\\n- Migrations are applied in a strict order to maintain consistency\\n\\n## Unified Storage Migration System (pkg/storage/unified/migrations/)\\n\\nA more modern migration framework for unified storage:\\n\\n**MigrationRegistry** (`registry.go`): Manages `MigrationDefinition` objects with:\\n- Resource-to-migrate specifications\\n- Per-organization migration execution\\n- Validator definitions for data integrity checks\\n- Migration ordering\\n\\n**UnifiedMigrator** (`migrator.go`): Executes migrations with:\\n- Per-organization isolation\\n- Streaming data processing with `BulkProcess`\\n- Retry logic and index rebuilding\\n- Progress tracking\\n\\n**MigrationRunner** (`resource_migration.go`): Executes per-organization logic for:\\n- Data transformation and validation\\n- Error handling with `ignoreErrors` option\\n- Auto-migration for small datasets\\n- Auto-rollback on failure\\n\\n**ResourceMigration** (`resource_migration.go`): Implements the SQL migration interface:\\n- Wraps `MigrationRunner` for integration with SQL migration pipeline\\n- Records results in `unifiedstorage_migration_log` table\\n- Skips re-execution if already completed\\n\\n**MigrationTableLocker** (`table_locker.go`): Prevents concurrent updates during migration:\\n- PostgreSQL: SELECT FOR UPDATE\\n- MySQL: LOCK TABLES\\n- SQLite: Transaction-based\\n\\n**Validators** (`validator.go`):\\n- `CountValidator`: Verifies record counts match between source and destination\\n- `FolderTreeValidator`: Validates folder hierarchy integrity\\n- `Validator` interface: Custom validation implementations\\n\\n## Secrets Migration Framework (pkg/services/secrets/migrator/)\\n\\nHandles encryption key rotation and secret re-encryption:\\n\\n**SecretsMigrator** (`migrator.go`):\\n- `ReEncryptSecrets()`: Decrypts and re-encrypts secrets with current encryption key\\n- `RollBackSecrets()`: Reverses to legacy encryption (implemented in `rollback.go`)\\n- Supports per-secret error handling without stopping the process\\n- Handles multiple secret types: simple secrets, JSON secrets, B64-encoded secrets\\n\\n**Rollback Implementation** (`rollback.go`): \\n- Type-specific rollback handlers (simpleSecret, jsonSecret, b64Secret, provisioningSecrets)\\n- Decrypts with new key, re-encrypts with legacy key\\n- Updates database records atomically\\n\\n**Provisioning Secrets** (`provisioning.go`):\\n- Handles datasource and webhook secret migrations\\n- Integrates with provisioning system\\n\\n## Secret Storage Migration (pkg/storage/secret/migrator/)\\n\\n**SecretDB** (`migrator.go`): Manages K8s-style secret storage migrations:\\n- `secret_keeper` table for secret references\\n- `secret_secure_value` table for encrypted values\\n- `secret_data_key` table for key management\\n- `secret_encrypted_value` table for migration tracking\\n- Implements `DatabaseMigrator` interface\\n- Runs migrations in isolated transaction via `RunMigrations()`\\n\\n## Legacy Secrets KVStore Migrations (pkg/services/secrets/kvstore/migrations/)\\n\\n**KVStore Migrator** (`migrator.go`): Handles legacy kvstore secret migrations\\n\\n**Datasource Migration** (`datasource_mig.go`):\\n- Migrates datasource passwords from kvstore\\n- Updates encryption for datasource secrets\\n- Handles backward compatibility\\n\\n## Version Tracking Tables\\n\\nEach migration system maintains its own version/log table:\\n- **migration_log**: Main Grafana schema migrations (columns: id, migration_id, sql, success, error, timestamp)\\n- **secret_migration_log**: Secrets manager migrations\\n- **resource_migration_log**: Unified storage resource migrations\\n- **unifiedstorage_migration_log**: Unified storage framework migrations\\n\\nThese tables prevent re-execution of completed migrations and record detailed execution history for debugging.\\n\\n## Rollback Handling\\n\\nRollback is implemented at multiple levels:\\n\\n1. **Secrets**: `RollBackSecrets()` in secrets/migrator reverses encryption state\\n2. **Unified Storage**: `ResourceMigration` implements auto-rollback on validation failure\\n3. **SQL Migrations**: Downtime migrations cannot be automatically rolled back; integrated systems for managing database schema changes across different storage backends and secret management layers.\\n\\n## Core SQL Store Migration System (pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/)\\n\\nThe foundation of Grafana's migration framework is implemented in `migrator.go`, which provides the `Migrator` type that orchestrates the execution of migrations. The migrator:\\n- Maintains a migration log table (`migration_log`, `secret_migration_log`, `resource_migration_log`, or `unifiedstorage_migration_log`) that tracks which migrations have been applied\\n- Executes migrations sequentially based on their dependencies\\n- Supports database locking to prevent concurrent migrations\\n- Records migration results including success/failure status and timestamps\\n\\nThe `types.go` file defines core interfaces:\\n- `Migration` interface: Base interface for all migrations with `SQL(dialect)`, `Id()`, and condition methods\\n- `CodeMigration` interface: For migrations that execute custom Go code via `Exec()` method\\n- `MigrationCondition` interface: For conditional migration execution\\n\\n## SQL Dialect Abstraction (MySQL/Postgres/SQLite)\\n\\nThe dialect abstraction layer (`dialect.go`) provides a `Dialect` interface with dialect-specific implementations:\\n- `BaseDialect` provides common functionality including SQL generation for CREATE TABLE, ADD COLUMN, CREATE INDEX, etc.\\n- `mysql_dialect.go`: MySQL-specific implementation with InnoDB engine, UTF8MB4 collation support, and MySQL-specific locking\\n- `postgres_dialect.go`: PostgreSQL implementation with native UUID support and PostgreSQL-specific syntax\\n- `sqlite_dialect.go`: SQLite implementation with transaction-based locking and PRAGMA support\\n\\nEach dialect implements:\\n- `Quote()`: identifier quoting specific to the database\\n- `SQLType()`: column type mapping\\n- `CreateTableSQL()`, `AddColumnSQL()`, `CreateIndexSQL()`: SQL generation\\n- `Lock()`/`Unlock()`: database-specific locking mechanisms\\n- `CreateDatabaseFromSnapshot()`: schema recreation from snapshot files\\n\\n## Migration Definitions and Types\\n\\n`migrations.go` provides migration builders:\\n- `RawSQLMigration`: Direct SQL execution\\n- `AddTableMigration`: Table creation with dialect-specific SQL generation\\n- `AddColumnMigration`: Add column operations\\n- `DropIndexMigration`, `DropTableMigration`, etc.\\n\\nEach migration type's `SQL(dialect)` method generates database-specific SQL statements.\\n\\n## OSS Migrations Registry (pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/)\\n\\nThe `OSSMigrations` type in `migrations.go` implements the `DatabaseMigrator` interface and aggregates all migrations by calling:\\n- `addUserMigrations()`, `addDashboardMigration()`, `addDataSourceMigration()`, etc.\\n- Each adds migrations to the `Migrator` instance\\n- Migrations are applied in a strict order to maintain consistency\\n\\n## Unified Storage Migration System (pkg/storage/unified/migrations/)\\n\\nA more modern migration framework for unified storage:\\n\\n**MigrationRegistry** (`registry.go`): Manages `MigrationDefinition` objects with:\\n- Resource-to-migrate specifications\\n- Per-organization migration execution\\n- Validator definitions for data integrity checks\\n- Migration ordering\\n\\n**UnifiedMigrator** (`migrator.go`): Executes migrations with:\\n- Per-organization isolation\\n- Streaming data processing with `BulkProcess`\\n- Retry logic and index rebuilding\\n- Progress tracking\\n\\n**MigrationRunner** (`resource_migration.go`): Executes per-organization logic for:\\n- Data transformation and validation\\n- Error handling with `ignoreErrors` option\\n- Auto-migration for small datasets\\n- Auto-rollback on failure\\n\\n**ResourceMigration** (`resource_migration.go`): Implements the SQL migration interface:\\n- Wraps `MigrationRunner` for integration with SQL migration pipeline\\n- Records results in `unifiedstorage_migration_log` table\\n- Skips re-execution if already completed\\n\\n**MigrationTableLocker** (`table_locker.go`): Prevents concurrent updates during migration:\\n- PostgreSQL: SELECT FOR UPDATE\\n- MySQL: LOCK TABLES\\n- SQLite: Transaction-based\\n\\n**Validators** (`validator.go`):\\n- `CountValidator`: Verifies record counts match between source and destination\\n- `FolderTreeValidator`: Validates folder hierarchy integrity\\n- `Validator` interface: Custom validation implementations\\n\\n## Secrets Migration Framework (pkg/services/secrets/migrator/)\\n\\nHandles encryption key rotation and secret re-encryption:\\n\\n**SecretsMigrator** (`migrator.go`):\\n- `ReEncryptSecrets()`: Decrypts and re-encrypts secrets with current encryption key\\n- `RollBackSecrets()`: Reverses to legacy encryption (implemented in `rollback.go`)\\n- Supports per-secret error handling without stopping the process\\n- Handles multiple secret types: simple secrets, JSON secrets, B64-encoded secrets\\n\\n**Rollback Implementation** (`rollback.go`): \\n- Type-specific rollback handlers (simpleSecret, jsonSecret, b64Secret, provisioningSecrets)\\n- Decrypts with new key, re-encrypts with legacy key\\n- Updates database records atomically\\n\\n**Provisioning Secrets** (`provisioning.go`):\\n- Handles datasource and webhook secret migrations\\n- Integrates with provisioning system\\n\\n## Secret Storage Migration (pkg/storage/secret/migrator/)\\n\\n**SecretDB** (`migrator.go`): Manages K8s-style secret storage migrations:\\n- `secret_keeper` table for secret references\\n- `secret_secure_value` table for encrypted values\\n- `secret_data_key` table for key management\\n- `secret_encrypted_value` table for migration tracking\\n- Implements `DatabaseMigrator` interface\\n- Runs migrations in isolated transaction via `RunMigrations()`\\n\\n## Legacy Secrets KVStore Migrations (pkg/services/secrets/kvstore/migrations/)\\n\\n**KVStore Migrator** (`migrator.go`): Handles legacy kvstore secret migrations\\n\\n**Datasource Migration** (`datasource_mig.go`):\\n- Migrates datasource passwords from kvstore\\n- Updates encryption for datasource secrets\\n- Handles backward compatibility\\n\\n## Version Tracking Tables\\n\\nEach migration system maintains its own version/log table:\\n- **migration_log**: Main Grafana schema migrations (columns: id, migration_id, sql, success, error, timestamp)\\n- **secret_migration_log**: Secrets manager migrations\\n- **resource_migration_log**: Unified storage resource migrations\\n- **unifiedstorage_migration_log**: Unified storage framework migrations\\n\\nThese tables prevent re-execution of completed migrations and record detailed execution history for debugging.\\n\\n## Rollback Handling\\n\\nRollback is implemented at multiple levels:\\n\\n1. **Secrets**: `RollBackSecrets()` in secrets/migrator reverses encryption state\\n2. **Unified Storage**: `ResourceMigration` implements auto-rollback on validation failure\\n3. **SQL Migrations**: Downtime migrations cannot be automatically rolled back; schema changes are managed through forward migrations only\\n\\nThe framework ensures migrations are idempotent and can be safely re-run, making gradual rollout and recovery possible.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
